# getCommonList

params ={'serviceKey' : '2xIM1IgBqXn+l2lfsQgsg6hNB7bu1CbSvubTbm/9Q42kTa9XZIsQaRPENls43Clf8PVz9/e3RRH4Uho6Zl6ijQ==', 'type' : 'json', 'groupCode' : '01', 'page' : '1', 'rowNum' : '10' }

# print(response.content)
print(response_CommonList.json())

# getAptlist

url = 'http://apis.data.go.kr/B552584/RfidFoodWasteServiceNew/getAptlist'
key = '2xIM1IgBqXn+l2lfsQgsg6hNB7bu1CbSvubTbm/9Q42kTa9XZIsQaRPENls43Clf8PVz9/e3RRH4Uho6Zl6ijQ=='

for city in CityCodeList:
    params ={'serviceKey' : key, 'type' : 'json', 'cityCode' : city,  'rowNum' : 180}
    response_Aptlist = requests.get(url, params=params)
    
    if CityCodeList.index(city) == 0:
        df_Aptlist = pd.DataFrame(response_Aptlist.json()['data']['list'])
        print(CityCodeList.index(city))
    else:
        temp_Aptlist = pd.DataFrame(response_Aptlist.json()['data']['list'])
        
        df_Aptlist = pd.concat([df_Aptlist, temp_Aptlist])
        
        print(CityCodeList.index(city))
# print(response.content)
# print(response_Aptlist.json())

print(df_Aptlist)

#  ()   
# getCityAptDayList

url = 'http://apis.data.go.kr/B552584/RfidFoodWasteServiceNew/getCityAptDayList'
key = '2xIM1IgBqXn+l2lfsQgsg6hNB7bu1CbSvubTbm/9Q42kTa9XZIsQaRPENls43Clf8PVz9/e3RRH4Uho6Zl6ijQ=='

for apt in All_AptCodes[944:]:
    params ={'serviceKey' : key, 'type' : 'json', 'disYear' : '2020', 'disMonth' : '03', 'cityCode' : apt[:3], 'aptCode' : apt, 'page' : '1', 'rowNum' : '1000'}
    response_CityAptDayList = requests.get(url, params=params)
# print(response.content)
#     print(response_CityAptDayList.json())
    
     
    if All_AptCodes.index(apt) == 0:
        df_All_AptDay = pd.DataFrame(response_CityAptDayList.json()['data']['list'])
        print(All_AptCodes.index(apt))
    else:
        try:
            temp_All_AptDay = pd.DataFrame(response_CityAptDayList.json()['data']['list'])

            df_All_AptDay = pd.concat([df_All_AptDay, temp_All_AptDay])

            print(All_AptCodes.index(apt))
        except:
            print(All_AptCodes.index(apt))
            print('')
        
    time.sleep(0.2)
# print(response.content)|
# print(response_Aptlist.json())

print(df_All_AptDay)

# getCityAptDayList

url = 'http://apis.data.go.kr/B552584/RfidFoodWasteServiceNew/getCityAptDayList'
key = '2xIM1IgBqXn+l2lfsQgsg6hNB7bu1CbSvubTbm/9Q42kTa9XZIsQaRPENls43Clf8PVz9/e3RRH4Uho6Zl6ijQ=='

for apt in JunSAptCodes:
    params ={'serviceKey' : key, 'type' : 'json', 'disYear' : '2020', 'disMonth' : '06', 'cityCode' : apt[:3], 'aptCode' : apt, 'page' : '1', 'rowNum' : '100000'}
    response_CityAptDayList = requests.get(url, params=params)
# print(response.content)
#     print(response_CityAptDayList.json())
    
     
    if JunSAptCodes.index(apt) == 0:
        df_JunSAptDay = pd.DataFrame(response_CityAptDayList.json()['data']['list'])
        print(JunSAptCodes.index(apt))
    else:
        try:
            temp_JunSAptDay = pd.DataFrame(response_CityAptDayList.json()['data']['list'])

            df_JunSAptDay = pd.concat([df_JunSAptDay, temp_JunSAptDay])

            print(JunSAptCodes.index(apt))
        except:
            print(JunSAptCodes.index(apt))
            print('')
        
    time.sleep(0.2)

# print(response_Aptlist.json())

print(df_JunSAptDay)

    params ={'serviceKey' : key, 'type' : 'json', 'disYear' : '2020', 'disMonth' : '06', 'cityCode' : apt[:3], 'aptCode' : apt, 'page' : '1', 'rowNum' : '100000'}

#  ()   
# getCityAptDayList

url = 'http://apis.data.go.kr/B552584/RfidFoodWasteServiceNew/getCityAptDayList'
key = '2xIM1IgBqXn+l2lfsQgsg6hNB7bu1CbSvubTbm/9Q42kTa9XZIsQaRPENls43Clf8PVz9/e3RRH4Uho6Zl6ijQ=='

for apt in GangAptCodes:
    params ={'serviceKey' : key, 'type' : 'json', 'disYear' : '2020', 'disMonth' : '06', 'cityCode' : apt[:3], 'aptCode' : apt, 'page' : '1', 'rowNum' : '100000'}
    response_CityAptDayList = requests.get(url, params=params)
# print(response.content)
#     print(response_CityAptDayList.json())
    
     
    if GangAptCodes.index(apt) == 0:
        df_GangAptDay = pd.DataFrame(response_CityAptDayList.json()['data']['list'])
        print(GangAptCodes.index(apt))
    else:
        try:
            temp_GangAptDay = pd.DataFrame(response_CityAptDayList.json()['data']['list'])

            df_GangAptDay = pd.concat([df_GangAptDay, temp_GangAptDay])

            print(GangAptCodes.index(apt))
        except:
            print(GangAptCodes.index(apt))
            print('')
        
    time.sleep(0.2)
# print(response.content)|
# print(response_Aptlist.json())

print(df_GangAptDay)

# getAptlist

url = 'http://apis.data.go.kr/B552584/RfidFoodWasteServiceNew/getAptlist'
key = '2xIM1IgBqXn+l2lfsQgsg6hNB7bu1CbSvubTbm/9Q42kTa9XZIsQaRPENls43Clf8PVz9/e3RRH4Uho6Zl6ijQ=='

for city in CityCodeList:
    params ={'serviceKey' : key, 'type' : 'json', 'cityCode' : city,  'rowNum' : 180}
    response_Aptlist = requests.get(url, params=params)
    
    if CityCodeList.index(city) == 0:
        df_Aptlist = pd.DataFrame(response_Aptlist.json()['data']['list'])
        print(CityCodeList.index(city))
    else:
        temp_Aptlist = pd.DataFrame(response_Aptlist.json()['data']['list'])
        
        df_Aptlist = pd.concat([df_Aptlist, temp_Aptlist])
        
        print(CityCodeList.index(city))
# print(response.content)
# print(response_Aptlist.json())

print(df_Aptlist)

# getCityAptDayList

url = 'http://apis.data.go.kr/B552584/RfidFoodWasteServiceNew/getCityAptDayList'
key = '2xIM1IgBqXn+l2lfsQgsg6hNB7bu1CbSvubTbm/9Q42kTa9XZIsQaRPENls43Clf8PVz9/e3RRH4Uho6Zl6ijQ=='

for apt in SeoulAptCodes[1184:]:
    params ={'serviceKey' : key, 'type' : 'json', 'disYear' : '2020', 'disMonth' : '05', 'cityCode' : apt[:3], 'aptCode' : apt, 'page' : '1', 'rowNum' : '100000'}
    response_CityAptDayList = requests.get(url, params=params)
# print(response.content)
#     print(response_CityAptDayList.json())
    
     
    if SeoulAptCodes.index(apt) == 0:
        df_SeoulAptDay05 = pd.DataFrame(response_CityAptDayList.json()['data']['list'])
        print(SeoulAptCodes.index(apt))
    else:
        try:
            temp_SeoulAptDay05 = pd.DataFrame(response_CityAptDayList.json()['data']['list'])

            df_SeoulAptDay05 = pd.concat([df_SeoulAptDay05, temp_SeoulAptDay05])

            print(SeoulAptCodes.index(apt))
        except:
            print(SeoulAptCodes.index(apt))
            print('')
        
    time.sleep(0.2)
# print(response.content)|
# print(response_Aptlist.json())

print(df_SeoulAptDay05)

# getCityAptDayList

url = 'http://apis.data.go.kr/B552584/RfidFoodWasteServiceNew/getCityAptDayList'
key = '2xIM1IgBqXn+l2lfsQgsg6hNB7bu1CbSvubTbm/9Q42kTa9XZIsQaRPENls43Clf8PVz9/e3RRH4Uho6Zl6ijQ=='

for apt in GgiAptCodes:
    params ={'serviceKey' : key, 'type' : 'json', 'disYear' : '2020', 'disMonth' : '06', 'cityCode' : apt[:3], 'aptCode' : apt, 'page' : '1', 'rowNum' : '100000'}
    response_CityAptDayList = requests.get(url, params=params)
# print(response.content)
#     print(response_CityAptDayList.json())
    
     
    if GgiAptCodes.index(apt) == 0:
        df_GgiAptDay = pd.DataFrame(response_CityAptDayList.json()['data']['list'])
        print(GgiAptCodes.index(apt))
    else:
        try:
            temp_GgiAptDay = pd.DataFrame(response_CityAptDayList.json()['data']['list'])

            df_GgiAptDay = pd.concat([df_GgiAptDay, temp_GgiAptDay])

            print(GgiAptCodes.index(apt))
        except:
            print(GgiAptCodes.index(apt))
            print('')
        
    time.sleep(0.2)

print(df_GgiAptDay)

#       
# getAptLocInfoList

url = 'http://apis.data.go.kr/B552584/RfidFoodWasteServiceNew/getAptLocInfoList'
key = '2xIM1IgBqXn+l2lfsQgsg6hNB7bu1CbSvubTbm/9Q42kTa9XZIsQaRPENls43Clf8PVz9/e3RRH4Uho6Zl6ijQ=='

for city in All_CityCodes:
    params ={'serviceKey' : key, 'type' : 'json', 'cityCode' : city, 'page' : '1', 'rowNum' : '1000'}


    response_CityAptLocInfoList = requests.get(url, params=params)
# print(response.content)
#     print(response_CityAptDayList.json())

    if All_CityCodes.index(city) == 0:
        df_AptLocInfoList = pd.DataFrame(response_CityAptLocInfoList.json()['data']['list'])
        print(All_CityCodes.index(city))
    else:
        try:
            temp_AptLocInfoList = pd.DataFrame(response_CityAptLocInfoList.json()['data']['list'])

            df_AptLocInfoList = pd.concat([df_AptLocInfoList, temp_AptLocInfoList])

            print(All_CityCodes.index(city))
        except:
            print()
            print(All_CityCodes.index(city), '')
            print()
        
    time.sleep(0.2)
# print(response.content)|
# print(response_Aptlist.json())

print(df_AptLocInfoList)
